      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 2nd century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 200 to 101 BC there were 237
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 80 were partial, 73 were annular (two
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 63 were total (one non-central), and 21 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 7 different years: 193 BC, 175 BC, 168 BC, 157 BC, 135 BC, 121 BC, and 117 BC.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

           Lists of eclipses

           <tr>
            <th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="width:1%">
             By century
            </th>
            <td class="navbox-list navbox-odd" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
             <div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
              <ul>
               <li>
                <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_in_antiquity" title="List of solar eclipses in antiquity">
                 Antiquity
                </a>
               </li>
               <li>

                 20th BC
                </a>
               </li>
               <li>
                <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_in_the_19th_century_BC" title="List of solar eclipses in the 19th century BC">
                 19th BC
                </a>
               </li>
               <li>

                 18th BC
                </a>
               </li>
               <li>
                <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_in_the_17th_century_BC" title="List of solar eclipses in the 17th century BC">
                 17th BC
                </a>
               </li>
               <li>
                <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_in_the_16th_century_BC" title="List of solar eclipses in the 16th century BC">
                 16th BC
                </a>
